   $env('loadBigDataHomepage', function() {
	var cookieId = "";
	var atgId = "";
	var zipCode = "";
	var storeNumber = "";
	var K_favstore = "";
	var K_favstoreSplit = "";
	
	
	if(Kjs.cookie.get("s_vi")!=null && Kjs.cookie.get("s_vi")!='')
	{
	cookieId = Kjs.cookie.get("s_vi");
	}
	if (Kjs.cookie.get("VisitorUsaFullName")!=null && Kjs.cookie.get("VisitorUsaFullName")!='')
	{
	if(Kjs.cookie.get("VisitorId")!=null && Kjs.cookie.get("VisitorId")!='')
	{
	atgId = Kjs.cookie.get("VisitorId");
	}
	}
	if(Kjs.cookie.get("K_favstore")!=null && Kjs.cookie.get("K_favstore")!=''){
	K_favstore = Kjs.cookie.get("K_favstore");
	K_favstoreSplit = K_favstore.split("|");
	if(K_favstoreSplit[0]){
	zipCode = K_favstoreSplit[0];
	}
	if(K_favstoreSplit[1]){
	storeNumber = K_favstoreSplit[1];
	}
	}
	var mcid = (typeof Visitor !='undefined')? Visitor.getInstance("F0EF5E09512D2CD20A490D4D@AdobeOrg") : '';
	var vId = (mcid ? mcid.getMarketingCloudVisitorID()  : '') ;
	
	var saleEventP1Valuesplit = "";
	var saleEventP1Value = "";
	var recommendationRenderer = bd.RecommendationRenderer.getInstance();	
	recommendationRenderer.setApiKey('NQeOQ7owHHPkdkMkKuH5tPpGu0AvIIOu')
	.setChannel('WebStore')
	.setPage('Home') 
	.setCcp('atgId', atgId)
	.setCcp('cookieId', cookieId)
	.setCcp('mcmId', vId)
	.setCcp('zipCode', zipCode) 
	.setCcp('storeNumber', storeNumber) 
	
	.onProductClick(bd.recommendationClickHandler)
	.injectCombinedRecommendations();
	
	Kjs.lazy.scrollBD(recommendationRenderer);
	});

     <script>
      /**
	 * Simple YouTube v1.0.3
	 */
	(function() {
		"use strict";

		/*///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
		// load the YouTube player API code asynchronously
		///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////*/
		var tag = document.createElement("script");
		tag.src = "https://www.youtube.com/iframe_api";
		var firstScriptTag = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
		firstScriptTag.parentNode.insertBefore(tag, firstScriptTag);
	})(); /* IIFE end */

	/*///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
	// when the API code is downloaded and ready
	///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////*/
	window.onYouTubeIframeAPIReady = (function() {
		"use strict";

		var kickstartSimpleYouTube = function() {
			/* autoplay variable */
			var autoPlay = true;

			/* needed for targeting player */
			var player = "";

			/* hide videoPoster */
			document
				.getElementById("hp-video-paused")
				.classList.add("is-hidden");

			/* Function to check if element is in viewport */
			var ytViewport = function(elem) {
				var bounding = elem.getBoundingClientRect();
				/* dither to allow for a little wiggle room on size/in view frame */
				var dither = 200;
				return (
					bounding.top + dither >= 0 &&
					bounding.left + dither >= 0 &&
					bounding.bottom - dither <=
					(window.innerHeight ||
						document.documentElement.clientHeight) &&
					bounding.right - dither <=
					(window.innerWidth + dither ||
						document.documentElement.clientWidth)
				);
			};

			var playVideo = function(player) {
				document
					.getElementById("hp-video-paused")
					.classList.add("is-hidden");
				document
					.getElementById("youtube-video-container")
					.classList.remove("is-hidden");
				if (player != "" && player != undefined) {
					player.playVideo();
				}
			};

			var pauseVideo = function(player) {
				document
					.getElementById("hp-video-paused")
					.classList.remove("is-hidden");
				document
					.getElementById("youtube-video-container")
					.classList.add("is-hidden");
				if (player != "" && player != undefined) {
					player.pauseVideo();
				}
			};

			/*///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
			// when the YouTube video is ready
			///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////*/
			var onPlayerReady = function(id) {
				/* get iframe */
				var iframe = document.getElementById(id);

				/* remove aria label */
				iframe.setAttribute("aria-label", "");

				/* add it to tab order */
				iframe.setAttribute("tabindex", 0);

				//* play inline
				iframe.setAttribute("webkit-playsinline", "1");

				/* give it a bit */
				var clickIt = setInterval(function() {
					/* get element again and then focus to the video */
					document.getElementById(id).focus();
					clearInterval(clickIt);
				}, 0);
			};

			/*///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
			// create iframe for video
			///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////*/
			var createIframe = function() {
				/* the item clicked */
				var target = this;

				/* retrieve YouTube ID */
				var youtubeId = target.dataset.youtube;

				/* and insert video player */
				/* eslint-disable */
				player = new YT.Player(target, {
					/* eslint-enable */
					videoId: youtubeId,
					height: 720,
					width: 1440,
					playerVars: {
						playsinline:1,
						fs:0,
						rel: 0,
						autoplay: 1,
						mute: 1,
						controls: 1,
						showinfo: 0,
						events: {
							onReady: onPlayerReady(this.id)
						}
					}
				});
			};

			/* find all cta's */
			var simpleYoutube = document.getElementsByClassName(
				"hp-video-link"
			);

			/* store how many cta's are available */
			var ctaCount = simpleYoutube.length;

			/* loop through each cta */
			for (var ctas = 0; ctas < ctaCount; ++ctas) {
				/* retrieve YouTube ID */
				var youtubeId = simpleYoutube[ctas].href.split(
					"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v="
				)[1];

				/*  retrieve class selectors */
				var classSelectors = simpleYoutube[ctas]
					.getAttribute("class")
					.replace(/hp-video-link/g, "");

				/* get html in anchor */
				var html = simpleYoutube[ctas].innerHTML;

				/*  get html in anchor */
				var description = simpleYoutube[ctas].getAttribute(
					"aria-label"
				);

				/* hide anchors */
				simpleYoutube[ctas].classList.add("is-hidden");

				/* add an accessible button */
				simpleYoutube[ctas].insertAdjacentHTML(
					"afterend",
					`<div id="youtube-video-container" class="simple-youtube__container"><div class="simple-youtube__container__zone"><button id="js-simple-youtube-${ctas}" class="${classSelectors}" data-youtube="${youtubeId}" aria-label="${description}">${html}</button></div></div>`
				);

				/* get new button */
				var button = document.getElementById(
					`js-simple-youtube-${ctas}`
				);

				/* and listen for user to click it */
				button.addEventListener("click", createIframe, false);

				/* if autoPlay, start the video process */
				if (autoPlay) {
					setTimeout(function() {
						button.click();
					}, 0);
				}

				/* Element to monitor */
				var ytVideo = document.querySelector("div.hp2__video__container");

				/* Fire function after page scrolling */
				window.addEventListener(
					"scroll",
					function playOnScroll() {
						/* If in viewport play the video */
						if (ytViewport(ytVideo)) {
							playVideo(player);
							if (/app/.test(window.location.host)) {
								window.removeEventListener("scroll", playOnScroll);
								/* pause video when it scrolls out of the viewport */
								window.addEventListener(
									"scroll",
									function(){
										if (!ytViewport(ytVideo)) {
											if (player != "" && player != undefined) {
												player.pauseVideo();
											}
										}
									}
								);
							}
						} else {
							pauseVideo(player);
						}
					},
					false
				);
			}
		}; /* end simpleYouTube */

		var stateCheck = setInterval(function() {
			if (document.readyState === "complete") {
				clearInterval(stateCheck);
				kickstartSimpleYouTube();
			}
		}, 500);
	})(); /* end onYouTubeIframeAPIReady */


	/* //////////////////////////////////////////////
	// OPEN AND CLOSE BANNER ON CLICK
	////////////////////////////////////////////// */
	function openCTA() {
		var x = document.getElementById("hp2__bkg__block");
		var y = document.getElementById("hp-video-min-copy");
		if (x.style.display === "none") {
			x.style.display = "flex";
			y.style.display = "none";
		} else {
			x.style.display = "none";
			y.style.display = "flex";
		}
	}
	function closeCTA() {
		var x = document.getElementById("hp2__bkg__block");
		var y = document.getElementById("hp-video-min-copy");
		if (y.style.display === "flex") {
			y.style.display = "none";
			x.style.display = "flex";
		} else {
			y.style.display = "flex";
			x.style.display = "none";
		}
	}
	/* end open/close function */
     </script>

      .hp2-creative .intimates-split-image-promo{width:100%;font-size:5vw;height:auto;display:-webkit-box;display:-ms-flexbox;display:flex;-webkit-box-orient:vertical;-webkit-box-direction:normal;-ms-flex-direction:column;flex-direction:column;position:relative}@media (min-width:1440px){.hp2-creative .intimates-split-image-promo{font-size:16px}}.hp2-creative .intimates-split-image-promo .intimates-split-image-promo__first-half,.hp2-creative      <script>
      (function() {
		'use strict';
		var glideBrands = document.querySelector('.glideOutfitbar');
		var glideOutfitbar = new Glide(".glideOutfitbar", {
			breakpoints:{800:{perView:2.1}},
			rewind:false,
		});
		var mq = window.matchMedia("(min-width: 800px)");
		function mediaQueryFunction(mq) {
			if (mq.matches) {
				glideOutfitbar.destroy();
			}
			else{
				glideOutfitbar.mount();
			}
		};
		mediaQueryFunction(mq); // Call listener function at run time
		mq.addListener(mediaQueryFunction); // Attach listener function on state changes
	})();
     </script>

    function getCookieByName(n) {
			if (document.cookie.length > 0) {
				var s = document.cookie.indexOf(n + "=");
				if (s != -1) {
					s = s + n.length + 1;
					var e = document.cookie.indexOf(";", s);
					if (e == -1) {
						e = document.cookie.length;
					}
					return unescape(document.cookie.substring(s, e));
				}
			}
			return "";
		}		
		var pagePostalCode = "N/A";
		if (getCookieByName("store_location")!=null && getCookieByName("store_location")!='')
		{
			pagePostalCode = getCookieByName("store_location");
		}
   </script>

						document.cookie = c_name + "=" + c_value + ";path=/;domain=" + domain;
					}			
					var LoginSuccess = getCookieByName("LoginSuccess");					
					var SCTrackingBean = new Object();
					SCTrackingBean.pageName = "Homepage";
					SCTrackingBean.pageType="Homepage";
					SCTrackingBean.siteSections= "Homepage|Homepage";
					SCTrackingBean.subSections= "Homepage";
					SCTrackingBean.subSectionsLevel2= "Homepage";
					SCTrackingBean.eVar86 = "68";
					SCTrackingBean.eVar87 = "hp19";

					if(LoginSuccess == "true"){
						SCTrackingBean.events="event39";
						setLoginSuccessCookie("LoginSuccess", "false", "1", domain1);						
					}else{
						SCTrackingBean.events="";					
					}	
					$(document).ready(function() {
							$(document).on('click',"div#rr_horizontal_product_recommendations_div_id a", function(event){
								  event.preventDefault();
								  var request = $(this).attr("href");
								  var productFindingMethod= 'pfm=rrrecs-home-hor';
								  var modifiedRequest = addUrlParam(request,productFindingMethod);
								  location.href = modifiedRequest;
							}); 
							function addUrlParam(url,parameter) {
								var modifiedURL = url;
									// appends using the encoded url charaters like %3F (?) , %26 (&) , %23 (#) etc
									if (url.indexOf(".jsp%3F") > -1) {
										if (url.indexOf("%23") > -1) {
											 var urlParts= url.split("%23");
											 var modifiedURL = urlParts[0]+"%26"+parameter+"%23"+urlParts[1];
										} else {
											var modifiedURL = url+"%26"+parameter;
										}
								   } else {
									   if (url.indexOf("%23") > -1) {
											 var urlParts= url.split("%23");
											 var modifiedURL = urlParts[0]+"%3F"+parameter+"%23"+urlParts[1];
										} else {
											var modifiedURL = url+"%3F"+parameter;
										}
								   }
								 return modifiedURL;
							}
					 });
   </script>

     !(function(t) {
		"use strict";

		function o() {
			var o = t.location.hostname;
			return /^(m|m-stage)\./.test(o) ? "mobile" : /^(mobile|tkpreview)\./.test(o) && $("#id_skStudio_Wrapper").length ? "tablet-skava" : /^(mobile|mobile-stage)\./.test(o) ? "tablet-mosaic" : "desktop";
		}

		function e() {
			var e = o();
			return "mobile" === e || "tablet-mosaic" === e ? t.kohlsUtils.isLoggedIn() : "tablet-skava" === e ? "" !== (document.cookie.match(/(?:skVisitorFullName=)(.*?)(?:;|$)/) || ["", ""])[1] : "" !== (document.cookie.match(
				/(?:VisitorUsaFullName=)(.*?)(?:;|$)/) || ["", ""])[1];
		}

		function i() {
			s.addClass("is-logged-in");
		}

		function a() {
			$(".js-footer-back-to-top").on("click", n);
		}

		function n(o) {
			o.preventDefault(), t.requestAnimationFrame(function() {
				$("html, body").animate({
					scrollTop: 0
				}, {
					complete: function() {
						l.focus();
					}
				});
			});
		}
		var s, l;
		$(function() {
			l = $('<div id="footer-top-of-page" tabindex="-1"></div>');
			(s = $(".footer-global")), $("body").prepend(l), a(), e() && i();
		});
	})(this);

     function getUrlVars() {
			    var vars = {};
				var url = window.location.href;
				url = decodeURIComponent(url); 
			    var parts = url.replace(/[?&]+([^=&]+)=([^&]*)/gi, function(m,key,value) {
			        vars[key] = value;
			    });
			    return vars;
			}
			var page_rr_ads = getUrlVars()["pfm"];

    <script type="text/javascript">
     function isNative() {
			var hasParam = location.search.indexOf("mobileAppUser=S") > -1
					|| location.search.indexOf("mobileAppUser=T") > -1, hasCookie = getCookieByName("mobileAppUser") !== "";
			return hasParam || hasCookie;
		}
		function isTabletDevice(cookieValue) {
			return cookieValue.indexOf("|T|") > -1;
		}
		function isMobile(cookieValue) {
			return cookieValue.indexOf("1") === 0 || isMobileDomain();
		}
		function isMobileDomain() {
			return location.host.split(".")[0].indexOf("m") === 0;
		}
		function getCookieByName(n) {
			if (document.cookie.length > 0) {
				var s = document.cookie.indexOf(n + "=");
				if (s != -1) {
					s = s + n.length + 1;
					var e = document.cookie.indexOf(";", s);
					if (e == -1) {
						e = document.cookie.length;
					}
					return unescape(document.cookie.substring(s, e));
				}
			}
			return "";
		}
		function setNativeCookie() {
			var domain = document.domain, numDots = domain.split(".");
			if (numDots.length === 3) {
				domain = "." + numDots[1] + "." + numDots[2];
			}
			setCookie("mobileAppUser", "true", "365", domain);
			function setCookie(c_name, value, exdays, domain) {
				var exdate = new Date(), c_value;
				exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate() + exdays);
				c_value = escape(value)
						+ ((exdays == null) ? "" : "; expires="
								+ exdate.toUTCString());
				document.cookie = c_name + "=" + c_value + ";path=/;domain="
						+ domain;
			}
		}
		if (typeof (suites) !== "undefined") {
			var multiSuite, standardSuite = suites.standard || "", mobileCookie = getCookieByName("mobile");

			if (isNative()) {
				multiSuite = standardSuite + "," + suites.native;
				setNativeCookie();
			} else if (isTabletDevice(mobileCookie)) {
				multiSuite = standardSuite + "," + suites.tablet;
			} else if (isMobile(mobileCookie)) {
				multiSuite = standardSuite + "," + suites.mobile;
			}
		}
    </script>
    <script type="text/javascript">
     var s_account = (typeof (multiSuite) !== "undefined") ? multiSuite	: "kohlscomprod";
    </script>

   <script>
    $ready(function _$ready_vnload($) {
            var ulsList = $("ul");
            var lstElement = ulsList.children("li[replace]");
            if (lstElement !== null || lstElement !== undefined) {
                var element = null
                  , child = null
                  , attrValue = "";
                lstElement.each(function(idx, li) {
                    element = $(li);
                    child = element.find('[child]').first();
                    attrValue = child.attr("child");
                    if (attrValue != null || attrValue !== undefined) {
                        element.attr("class", attrValue);
                    }
                    child.removeAttr("child");
                    element.removeAttr("replace");
                });
            }
        });
        $ready(function _$ready_after_vnload($) {
            Kjs.poll(200, function() {
                return $('.vn-content a').length > 0;
            }, function() {
                var temp = $('.vn-content a');
                $.each(temp, function(i, v) {
                    var url = $(v).attr('data-url');
                    if (window.browseSearchPlatform != undefined) {
                        switch (window.browseSearchPlatform) {
                        case 'E':
                            url = updateParameterByName(url, 'srp', 'e1');
                            break;
                        case 'S':
                            url = updateParameterByName(url, 'srp', 'e2');
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                    $(v).attr('data-url', url);
                });
            });
        }, {
            isAfterReady: true
        });
   </script>
